The temporary office is located in the office of the Ministry of Railways on the first floor of Sassoon House on Nanjing Road. At 10:00 AM and 3:00 PM every day, all representatives will hold meetings to decide on leadership groups for hosting and visiting. The groups will be divided into five groups: economic, electrical, metallurgical and mining, civil engineering, and mechanical engineering. Each group will be assigned representatives: the economic group includes Jin Jingyang, Zhang Xinhua, Xie Baoqiao, and Zhou Zechun; the electrical group includes Zhuang Zhihuan and Tan Boyu; the metallurgical and mining group includes Hu Shuhua and Yang Gongzhao; the civil engineering group includes Shen Junyi and Zhu Chongguang; and the mechanical engineering group includes Xu Shanxiang and Xu Peihuang. Mr. Jin Jingyang has been appointed to handle all external liaison matters.

The Shanghai Special City Government has received an order from the central government to properly host the group. Mayor Zhang hosted a welcome reception for the group at the Dahua Hotel at 12:00 PM on the 10th and invited representatives from various central ministries and commissions to accompany him. It is reported that this banquet was specially held to introduce the group to the representatives of various ministries and commissions, so the hosts and guests only exchanged brief greetings and there were no formal speeches. The banquet ended happily around 3:00 PM.

Yixian Warship's Launching Ceremony Yesterday 131

Chen Shaokuan's Talk in Shanghai. The launching ceremony of the Yixian warship built by the Navy Department was held at the Gaochangmiao Jiangnan Shipbuilding Factory shipyard at 9:00 AM yesterday. Chen Shaokuan, the Deputy Minister of Naval Affairs, came to Shanghai by train from Beijing to attend. After the meeting at 9:00 AM, about 50 people attended, including Chen Shaokuan, Chen Xunyong, Ma Deji, the Yixian warship construction section of the Shanghai Naval Disarmament Office, and the Jiangnan Shipbuilding Factory personnel. The ceremony order was quite simple. First, the workers placed the keel (that is, the steel plate at the bottom of the ship) in place. Chen Shaokuan personally held the iron hammer and installed the first cap nail. The second nail was hammered by Chen Xunyong, commander of the training fleet. Then, photos were taken, and the ceremony ended. A reporter from the Guowen News Agency went at 8:00 AM yesterday morning, was able to participate in the ceremony, and met with Chen Shaokuan. When asked about national affairs and the defense situation of the Yangtze River, the talk he received is recorded on the left. (Reporter of Guowen News Agency asked) Bangbu went to Fujian Provincial Party Committee members Lin Zhiyuan, Zheng Bao, Chen Naiyuan, Xu Xianshi, Cheng Shiyun, and Public Security Bureau Director Wu Shu and other six people, recently there are rumors of being killed, has the sir heard of it? (Chen replied) I have not heard of it, I am afraid there is not necessarily this fact. (Asked) Since there has not been an incident, where are the Lin group members imprisoned, and how will Minister Yang solve this matter? Has the rest of the solution been decided? (Answer) After Lin Zhiyuan and other members were escorted back from Hongshan Bridge, they were probably held in Youxi or Yanping. As for solving the Fujian issue, it is a prerequisite that Lu will first release the Fujian Committee members. Minister Yang should follow the central government's plan, even if Lu does violate it, the central government will have its own methods to deal with it. Will it tend to a military solution? (Answer) Not necessarily, because the Fujian change cannot be compared to the Northwest Yan-Feng rebellion this time, and the scope is small, so the central government does not want to rush to suppress it. The reason for slowly proceeding is also this, and when there is a method, it will still be handled in a mild manner. (Asked) Has the list of committee members for reorganizing the Fujian Provincial Government been internally determined? After Minister Yang comes to Shanghai, will the Fujian affairs be handled by Commander Chen Jiliang? Is it true that Chen will succeed the Chairman of Fujian? (Answer) I have not heard of Commander Chen Jiliang as Chairman of Fujian. I have not heard of the central government's decision or proposal on the selection of Fujian Committee members. The routine affairs of Fujian Province seem to be handled by the Provincial Government. (Asked) What is Minister Yang's condition like, and will he return to Fujian recently? Is he recuperating at Hongqiao Hospital, or is he recuperating at a residence on Avenue Joffre in this city? (Answer) Minister Yang's return to Fujian is undecided. What he is suffering from is hemoptysis, and he is currently recuperating at a relative's house in this city. (Asked) With the situation unstable, what is the navy's defense on the Yangtze River? (Answer) Military ships are stationed along the Yangtze River from Yichang in the west to Wusong in the east, in various ports such as Shashi, Xindi, Hankou, Anqing, Nanjing, and Tongzhou. Although there were bandits disturbing Xindi, Madang, Nantong, etc., they have now been pacified after being suppressed by the navy. All the captured bandits have also been sent to the local defense army for legal proceedings, so the defense is very strict. (Asked) When will you return to Beijing? (Answer) I have to return to Beijing tonight. At this point, because Chen was going to the Jiangnan Shipbuilding Factory to contact the Yixian ship, he said goodbye.

Recently, he has also followed the special chapter formulated and promulgated by the Ministry to implement the reorganization, which will be completed before April 13. It is heard that the content of the reorganization is to eliminate the personnel, compilation, and transportation departments that are not listed in the special chapter, as well as the titles of assistant, deputy section chief, and clerk. Also, the small number of people in the bureau who are nominally paid but have no work will be suspended in order to comply with the Ministry's chapter and save expenses. As for the original employees of other departments and sections, they will not be changed. The insect disaster of the old year was even worse. The southwest two villages are all white land, and no rice has been harvested. At present, the people are eating grass roots and bark. Some families have starved to death, and some wives cry because their children are hungry, and family members use their assets to seek death in lonely temples. There are cases where parents-in-law starved to death and daughters-in-law committed suicide, leaving only orphaned children. As for selling children, it is impossible to count. The wailing is everywhere, and the scene is full of trauma. The miserable scene is not what paper and ink can describe.

The victims of Taiwan and Wen are fortunate to be blessed and spared from the ravines. opened a relief association in the whole township and sent representatives to Shanghai to petition your association. I beg your association to promote benevolence and rain down in time to save the dying people.

Industry Mergers Cannot Be Changed 152

If There Are Any Questions, Please Ask the Party Department for Explanation

The Chamber of Commerce Reform Committee previously stipulated in the Law on Industrial and Commercial Guilds that only one guild is allowed to be established in the same area in the same industry. However, the groups in various industries in this city, or due to customary historical relations, have been divided into two groups in one industry for a long time. Once they are merged according to law, they are afraid that disputes will occur. In the organization and reorganization procedures of the Industrial and Commercial Guilds, it is stipulated that, according to custom and history, it is not necessary to force them to merge, and report to the central government for filing. The Central Party Department's Order No. 2128 stated that there is no legal basis for the above, and the commutation measures should be deleted immediately. After the Association complied with the order to delete, it still retained in the fourth paragraph of the procedure: "But if the nature of its business does have unmergeable parts, after investigation, it may be changed as appropriate." The case was reported to the central government, and now the Central Training Department's Order No. 2258 opened, "After investigation, the proviso of this paragraph conflicts with the first paragraph's stipulation that industrial organizations should strictly abide by Article 5 of the Law on Industrial and Commercial Guilds, "The establishment of guilds in the same industry in the same region shall be limited to one guild."

It should be deleted by itself. Those who still have questions about whether the nature of the business should be merged into an organization should submit a request to the Party Department for explanation."

Provincial Order to Reorganize the Baoshan Security Corps 154

Wu Jia, the magistrate of Baoshan County, received an order from the Suzhou People's Department to order the entire county's security corps to be handled in accordance with the new regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Interior. After Wu County Magistrate received the order, he convened all the district security corps chiefs at the county government for a meeting at 1:00 PM yesterday. Wu County Magistrate presided over the meeting and said that, according to the first order, the organization of the security corps based on the new regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Interior should be reorganized in accordance with the current security corps in order to emphasize the law. After a long discussion, the following measures were agreed upon: (1) The security corps in the five major districts of the county will be reorganized at the same time. (2) The number of security corps members and volunteers and the required funds in each district, (3) Compile the total number and funds, (4) The total number of military supplies such as guns and clothing,

(5) The steps to fundamentally reorganize, and the leaders of the group headquarters will handle them in accordance with the law. (6) Estimate the expenses after the reorganization, and the meeting will adjourn.

New National Anti-Drug Patrol Plan 157

The China National Anti-Drug Association launched a national anti-drug campaign last spring, dividing the country into several regions, with each region containing several key cities. The campaign was conducted sequentially, starting on April 1st with an opening ceremony in Shanghai, followed by a pilot program in the Zhejiang region, including Suzhou, Hangzhou, Ningbo, and Wenzhou, in addition to Shanghai itself. In the Yangtze River region, the campaign took place in Nanchang, Jiujiang, Anqing, and Wuhu, followed by the Northeast region in Shenyang, Harbin, and Jilin. Each location's campaign lasted from three to seven days, totaling twelve locations. Over five hundred organizations participated, and more than 350,000 people were involved. The impact of the campaign was far-reaching, effectively promoting discussion, awakening the public, and urging the government to take action. Last month, the Zhejiang Anti-Drug Branch carried out a province-wide patrol, assisted by personnel dispatched by the Association, leading to significant achievements. The Association has decided to continue the campaign in the remaining Central China, North China, South China, and West China regions to achieve the universal goal of nationwide anti-drug efforts. The dates, locations, and plans are detailed below: (1) Dates: Starting in the summer of the 19th year of the Republic of China (2) Locations: Central China: Wuchang, Hankou, Changsha, Yuezhou, Kaifeng, Zhengzhou; North China: Qingdao, Jinan, Tianjin, Beiping, Shijiazhuang, Taiyuan; South China: Fuzhou, Xiamen, Shantou, Guangzhou, Macau, Hong Kong, Wuzhou, Nanning; West China: Sichuan, Guizhou, Yunnan (3) Objectives and Measures: A. Awaken the public to work together to combat drugs. 1. Connect with local media organizations to promote the cause. B. Urge the government to effectively ban opium. 1. Strictly investigate the trafficking, sale, and use of drugs. 2. Petition the government to effectively ban opium. C. Respond to the International Opium Conference. 1. Investigate the drug situation. 2. Send telegrams to express public determination. 3. Request signatures for petitions. D. Hold an anti-drug exhibition, with exhibits categorized into ten areas: 1. Charts; 2. Slogans; 3. Slides; 4. Photographs; 5. Publications of the Association; 6. Narcotics; 7. Films; 8. Statues; 9. Forms; 10. Reports on the Association's achievements. E. Organize anti-drug branches and comrades' societies: 1. Convene joint meetings of various organizations; 2. Establish regulations for organizing anti-drug branches; 3. Recruit comrades to join; 4. Organize student comrades' societies; 5. Establish work plans; 6. Promote and sell anti-drug monthly magazines. This plan has been approved by the Association's Standing Committee and assigned to the secretariat for implementation. The secretariat is currently actively preparing.

Page 15

Local News 2

Yesterday 160

Hailstorms Hit Shanghai Twice

Water Accumulated into Ditches in a Short Time

Wing On Company Builds Small Dam

Two Merchant Ships Unable to Enter Port

Shanghai-Nanjing Flights Suspended

In recent days, the climate in Shanghai has been changing rapidly, with continuous rain and wind. Although the Cold Food Festival has just passed, it feels like the plum rain season. Yesterday morning, as the sun rose and shone brightly, people thought the weather would clear up. However, in an instant, dark clouds gathered, and the air became stuffy and humid, threatening rain. Thus, the weather alternated between rain and clearing, without stopping all morning. Half an hour before noon, suddenly dark clouds filled the sky, and most people waited expectantly, thinking that heavy rain would fall at any moment. But the rain god did not come for a long time, and the sky became darker and darker, the gloomy atmosphere gradually intensifying. Noon suddenly turned dark, almost like dusk. At 12:00 noon, it was like 6:00 or 7:00 in the evening.

Rain and Hail: The exact time of the daytime darkness was 12:03 PM, and it gradually recovered after about five or six minutes. The sunlight was reborn, and coarse raindrops fell like ink, mixed with hail. For a moment, the roof tiles all rattled, and the raindrops and hail pattered and tinkled on the glass windows, creating a clear and pleasant sound, like large and small pearls falling on a jade plate. After three or four minutes, the hail stopped and the rain fell, as heavy as the sky pouring down, cascading. In an instant, the water on the ground was ankle-deep, and the sewers could not drain the water in time, so they overflowed. This lasted for about forty-five minutes before it stopped.

Roads Flooded: During the heavy rain, low-lying areas turned into swamps. There were few pedestrians on both sides of the roads. The area around Yisheng Building on Nanjing Road is low-lying, and the Wing On Company was flooded like a ditch, making it difficult for customers to walk. The entrance facing Yinghua Street was severely affected by the flood, and an emergency measure had to be taken to build a temporary dam to prevent water from entering. The situation was quite serious, as can be seen. The rain subsided slightly after about forty-five minutes.

Ill-Fated Peach Blossoms: Around the Qingming Festival, on Longhua Road, people in silk clothes and hats flocked to the area to swing and stroll. Unfortunately, the weather was unfavorable, with rain on two out of three days, which disappointed pedestrians. Yesterday, the buses going directly to Longhua were deserted. The beautiful peach blossoms and weeping willows were devastated by the heavy rain, which was a great disappointment.

River Enshrouded in Mist: Yesterday, during the heaviest rain, the Huangpu River became a cloud of smoke. It was difficult to see across the river. Small boats and cargo lighters on the river dared not venture out and remained at the docks to avoid the rain. The river was deserted, with very few boats sailing, which was unprecedented.

Lightning Strikes Poles: Yesterday, thunder and lightning struck, with continuous rumbling sounds. It was reported that two telephone poles in front of the Sanbei Factory on Longhua Road were struck by lightning and split in two, and the power lines also fell to the ground. However, the power company sent workers to repair them soon after. It was also reported that three telephone poles near Tianbao Li on Haining Road were knocked down by lightning, causing considerable damage to the power lines. Workers were sent to repair them on the same day.

Loading and Unloading Halted: The stevedores at the various docks stopped working yesterday due to the heavy rain. Cargo lighters were also unable to open their hatches, which delayed the export of merchant ships.

Two Ships Detained by Fog: China Merchants Steam Navigation Company received a telegram from the Guangji, stating that it encountered heavy rain and fog near Zhoushan and had to anchor temporarily. The Haiyan also telegraphed that it encountered heavy rain and fog after leaving Wenzhou and had to anchor temporarily, delaying its arrival in Shanghai. Flights Suspended: The Shanghai-Chengdu Aviation Administration of the Ministry of Communications suspended flights to Nanjing yesterday morning because the sky had not cleared, the weather had suddenly become hot, and there was light fog, which indicated that it would rain. Around noon, black clouds covered the sky, and heavy rain fell soon after. If the weather is clear today, flights will resume as usual.

Dramatic Murder of Father by Kidnapper

Unexpected Encounter 161

Having Worn Out Shoes Searching in Vain

Found Without Any Effort

Wan Guoxiang, Full of Evil,

Cannot Escape in Front of the City God Temple

In the eighth month of the lunar calendar last year, a kidnapping and murder case occurred in Wanjiatun, a village in the northern part of Wuwei County, Anhui Province. The victim was shot and killed while resisting the kidnappers, who then demanded a ransom. The victim's fate remains unknown. The Wuwei County government later learned that the main perpetrator had fled to Shanghai and dispatched police officers to Shanghai twice to apprehend him, but to no avail. The six police officers stayed for a long time and ran out of funds. They were planning to return to Wuwei today to report back when they unexpectedly encountered the perpetrator while taking shelter from the rain in the City God Temple. They arrested him. Although the matter is minor, the situation is quite unusual. The details of the case are recorded below:

Kidnapping Son and Killing Father: Wan Zhikuan, a native of Wanjiatun, a village in the northern part of Wuwei County, Anhui Province, was a farmer by trade. He owned more than 300 mu of fertile land and was known as a local wealthy man. As a result, he came to the attention of bandits. Wan and his wife, Mrs. Wang, were an elderly couple over forty years old. They had a son named Xiaodai, whom they cherished as the apple of their eye. He was twelve years old. On the night of the fourteenth day of the eighth lunar month last year, more than ten bandits suddenly came and kidnapped Xiaodai. Wan was shot and killed by the bandits while trying to protect his beloved son.

Cousin is the Main Perpetrator: The case caused a sensation throughout the county. Zhang Siwei, the magistrate of Wuwei County, attached great importance to the case and ordered all police agencies in the county to solve it within a limited time. After several months, only five suspects were arrested. After repeated investigations, it was learned that the main perpetrator was Wan Guoxiang, the cousin of the kidnapped child. However, he had long fled to Shanghai, and his address was unknown. Magistrate Zhang dispatched police officer Xuan Wencheng to Shanghai to investigate and arrest him, no matter what.

Unexpected Encounter: Police officer Xuan and five colleagues arrived in Shanghai and stayed at the home of a friend at 40 Malan Road in the French Concession. They searched separately all day long. After more than ten days, there was no trace of him. The funds they had prepared were about to run out, and they planned to return to Wuwei to report back today. Yesterday morning, police officer Xuan and his colleagues went to the City God Temple to sightsee. After sightseeing, they planned to exit through the Fangbang Road gate when heavy rain suddenly began to pour down. Police officer Xuan and his colleagues took shelter from the rain in front of the temple gate. After a while, a man came, wearing a gray cloth shirt and a felt hat, and went straight to the front of the temple, exclaiming about the heavy rain. Police officer Xuan and his colleagues were watching the rain when they suddenly heard a familiar accent. Everyone looked at him, and it was none other than Wan Guoxiang, the main perpetrator of the kidnapping and murder!

Perpetrator's Confession: Police officer Xuan and his colleagues were overjoyed to see Wan Guoxiang and immediately arrested him. They took him to the First District, Second Precinct and presented the facts of the case and the writ. Chief Gao questioned the suspect. According to his confession, he was thirty-two years old and used to be engaged in the rice and wood business. Wan Zhikuan was his uncle. His father was named Baocheng and was the eldest son. He denied shooting his uncle and kidnapping his cousin. He said that he left his hometown on the thirteenth day of the ninth lunar month last year and told his aunt, Mrs. Wang, that he was going to his wife's family in Changzhou. He came to Shanghai once on the twentieth day of the same month and returned to Changzhou in mid-October. He had only been in Shanghai for two days this time. After hearing the confession, Chief Gao, considering the seriousness of the case, prepared a document and sent it to the Judicial Section for punishment that evening.

Liang and Yuan Disappear Simultaneously

Even Their Families Have Moved Away Completely

Honest People Cannot Be Trusted

Liang Reportedly Took a Ship to Hong Kong

Liang Shuxian, the chief revenue officer, and Yuan, a revenue officer of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Accounts Office, suddenly disappeared on Tuesday with 100,000 yuan. Duke, the traffic superintendent of the railway, reported the case to the Public Concession Police the night before. According to Duke, the money was the cash revenue of the railway bureau on Monday and was discovered missing on Wednesday morning. Liang had been working for the railway bureau for more than ten years and was known to be honest. Liang and Yuan did not come to the office yesterday morning, which aroused suspicion. The authorities sent people to their homes, only to find that they had moved away completely. Yuan had not been in office for long and had been recommended by someone. It is rumored that Liang left Shanghai yesterday on the Dollar Line's President Lincoln, but this has not been confirmed. Lake Bandits Rampant

Increasing Number of Refugees 163

More Than a Hundred People Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

Due to the rampant lake bandits who come and go without a trace, the towns of Weiting, Zhengyi, Waikuatang, Bacheng, Jiaozhi, Chenmu, etc., along the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway's Suzhou-Shanghai section, are experiencing multiple scares a day. Those with a little property in these towns are bringing their families to Shanghai and Suzhou to take temporary refuge. When the Shanghai-Nanjing slow train arrived at the North Station yesterday, it carried more than a hundred refugees from various towns and cities. They either stayed in hotels or went to relatives' homes for temporary shelter.

Tragic Inheritance Dispute

Brother Shoots Brother 164

Over 40 Mu of Fertile Land

Five Shots Fired, Blood Flowing Freely

Zhu Laowu, a deceased farmer from Zhujia Zhai, Twenty-Eighth Bao, Nineteenth Tu, West of Xujiahui Town, Shanghai, had two sons and one daughter: Wenming, 32 years old, and Aru, 29 years old, who are both married. After Laowu died, he left more than 40 mu of fertile land that had not yet been divided. As a result, the two brothers quarreled over the inheritance countless times. Although relatives and friends repeatedly tried to persuade them, neither would back down. Wenming harassed Aru again the night before, leading to a fight. However, Aru was very strong, and Wenming suffered minor injuries, harboring resentment in his heart. The next day, he borrowed a pistol from a friend in Xujiahui, intending to take revenge. He encountered Aru returning from a tomb sweeping ceremony in front of Anguo Temple (only a hundred yards from home). They met on a narrow road, and Wenming, consumed by anger, pulled out his gun and fired five shots, hitting Aru's left waist, leg, right arm, etc. Blood flowed freely, and he fell to the ground.

Patrolman Pan Xueceng from the Hongqiao Town Police Station of the First Precinct of the Sixth District heard the news and rushed to the scene. He saw that the injured person was covered in blood and was a terrible sight. The murderer had fled without a trace. After being identified by the villagers, the patrolman reported the incident to the family. Patrolman Pan sent the injured Zhu Aru to the Red Cross Hospital on Haige Road for treatment. His injuries were said to be serious, and his life was in danger. After learning of the incident, Chief Wang Xixiang personally inspected the scene of the incident and ordered all patrolmen to strictly arrest the murderer and bring him to justice.

Based on Report from Rickshaw Puller

Three More People Involved Arrested

Taken to Court for Trial Yesterday Morning

Deceased Confirmed as Liu Yiqing

Ge Wencheng is a Young Boy

On the morning of April 8th, a disturbance occurred on Beijing Road. A patrolman shot and killed one person and arrested eight workers and students. The details of the case have been reported twice in this newspaper after interrogation by the Special District Local Court and the Jiangsu Higher Court Branch. The name of the deceased was initially rumored to be Liu Yiqing, but the police could not confirm it at the time due to incomplete investigation. However, the police, including Detective Shen Chongli, Detective Hua Youshan, Detective Xu Decheng, and Western Detective Bibu from the Gordon Road Police Station, arrested Ge Wencheng, Peng Zijie, and Huang Peng the day before yesterday afternoon, confirming that the deceased was Liu Yiqing without a doubt. At the same time, the detectives also seized a large number of military weapons and various reactionary printed materials and books. According to the crime of illegal possession of military weapons, the case should be handled by the Special District Local Court.

However, since the case involves counter-revolutionary acts, it should be handled by the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court. The police first brought the case to the Special District Local Court yesterday morning. Judge Sun Yuan of the Criminal Division of the court approved the transfer of the case to the Higher Court Branch for investigation.

The police filed charges and transferred the entire case and witnesses to the Higher Court Branch at 2:00 PM. At that time, there were five other criminals detained with me. This matter was planned by Qian,

I was fooled by him. As for Zhu Guoliang, he discussed and contacted Qian after the incident, etc. When questioned, Zhu Guoliang confessed that he also worked in the lead printing department of the Commercial Press and did not know Chen or Qian,

nor did he have any grudges. This time, I was falsely accused. Qian Yiqing confessed,

"According to Chen, I contacted the plaintiff on the 26th, but on that day, I went to the Yixing District Party Headquarters to discuss the opening of a hospital and stayed there. I did not return to Shanghai by car until 10 PM on the 28th and went straight to the Daxin Hotel to find a friend.

I was arrested by detectives as soon as I stepped onto the escalator. As for in the patrol房 prison, I did say to Chen, 'I have no grudges against you, why did you falsely accuse me?'" When Shi Maoni was questioned, her confession was ambiguous. Finally, the criminals Wang Zongxiang and Zhang Jinrong were brought to the case to prove that Qian did say to Chen in prison, "Don't accuse me,

otherwise, I will hire a lawyer to have you shot," etc. After Judge Sun verified the confession,

because it was past noon, he ordered the defendants to be detained and postponed the hearing to Monday afternoon next week.

Circumnavigating the Globe by Wooden Boat 167

Stevenson's Ambition

Wenhui News reported that Stevenson, the second mate of the Yihua Yixing Steamship Company, now plans to circumnavigate the globe in a wooden sailboat named the Maxky, which was specially built and is currently docked in Shantou. Mr. Stevenson went to Hong Kong on the Yixing Steamship last week and then went to Shantou.

He will set sail on the boat at the end of this week or the beginning of next week,

Telephone Installation in Meilong Town Pending 168

Meilong Town in this city is located in western Shanghai and is the western gateway to the urban area, which is extremely important for defense. Moreover, it is still six miles away from Caohejing Town. Once there is an alarm, the response is slow. Therefore, the local people are eager to have company telephones installed. Convenient communications are not only beneficial to defense but also greatly beneficial to the development of the commercial market. The Second Direct District Branch of the Municipal Executive Committee in that area, in view of this, submitted a request to the Secretariat of the Municipal Executive Committee in February of this year, which was forwarded to the Municipal Public Works Bureau,

requesting that telephones be installed for public use. The bureau immediately forwarded the request to the Shanghai Telephone Bureau for verification. It is now known that after the Telephone Bureau's survey, the town is located far away and requires 200 telephone poles. In addition to borrowing telegraph poles, 20 poles need to be planted,

costing 600 yuan, and five measures are proposed: (1) This line

must wait until the components of the West Branch Bureau are installed before a solution can be found. (2) Whether the telegraph poles can be borrowed must be agreed upon by the Telegraph Bureau. (3) There must be reputable shops in the town willing to be responsible for acting as retailers of telephones, and the method of communication can be negotiated with the bureau. (4) How much of the construction cost can the town contribute? (5) The bureau can provide considerable remuneration for acting as a public telephone. There are still many problems with the installation of telephones in Meilong Town, and it is difficult to achieve it in the short term.

Municipal Public Works Bureau and Fruit Industry 169

Signed a Contract to Build a Wharf

The Industry to Undertake the Construction Costs

The Municipal Public Works Bureau originally planned to operate a ferry between the Muddy River Crossing in Pudong and the Shiliupu in Puxi, and decided to use the Shiliupu manure removal wharf as the ferry terminal. Subsequently, the Fruit Industry Association, Shixingtang, also

requested to lease the site to build a fruit boat wharf. The five bureaus of Finance, Public Works, Land, Health, and Public Works jointly decided that after the manure removal wharf was relocated, the entire site would be managed by the Public Works Bureau to build the municipal ferry construction wharf. All the remaining parts that do not conflict with the municipal ferry would be designated by the Public Works Bureau and distributed to the industry for use. The cost of the ferry terminal construction would be borne by the industry. After the Public Works Bureau estimated and repeatedly discussed, it was set at 5,000 taels. Later, the industry requested to change the regulations and build a floating bridge along the shoreline. The Public Works Bureau allowed this and simultaneously proposed that all the wharves and the revetment within the wharf area should be entirely borne by the industry, and the association also agreed to undertake this. The Public Works Bureau then negotiated and signed a contract to build the wharf. On January 21 of this year, the bureau invited all parties concerned to discuss the draft contract. The industry representatives present had no objections to the conditions offered. The draft contract was then submitted to the municipal government for approval.

Yesterday (the 10th) at 2 PM, the bureau invited the industry representatives to the bureau to formally sign the contract. All the 5,000 taels for the ferry terminal construction subsidy and the 2,000 yuan for the revetment subsidy were also paid by the representative together.

Asiatische Gesellschaft Building to Be Renovated 170

The Zi Lin News reported that the Asiatische Gesellschaft building was built 60 years ago. It has been infested by worms and termites, and the wood is decaying. It is now beyond repair. In the past two years, it was decided to raise 100,000 taels to rebuild a new

building for use as a library, museum, and assembly hall. A committee was then organized to raise funds. After two years, only 750 yuan has been raised. It was not until this Monday that Mr. Gu generously donated 500 taels. Therefore, the committee was reorganized last month to actively proceed with fundraising, contacting the Public Works Bureau and various banks. According to the

society's purpose, it specializes in studying China and the Far East.

The library has 12,000 volumes, many of which are rare books. The museum is open to the public for reading. The land was allocated by the British government and is now worth 10,000 pounds. If funding is sufficient for the new building plan,

it is planned to build a five-story building. In addition to serving as a library, museum, assembly hall, art gallery, and document and book storage rooms, the rest will be rented out.

Commercial and Political Committee 171

Please Restore Traffic on Hankou Road

Affecting Business Operations on the Road

The Commercial and Political Committee sent a letter to the Public Works Bureau yesterday, requesting the restoration of traffic on Hankou Road, stating, "On the 10th of this month, we received a joint letter from the businesses on Hankou Road stating that since the Public Works Bureau designated Hankou Road traffic as one-way from April 1, the movement of vehicles has been restricted, and the business operations on this road have been greatly reduced. Moreover, the one-way rule is from 8:00 AM to 9:30 AM and from 1:00 PM to 2:30 PM, from west to east, and from 12:00 PM to 1:00 PM and from 4:00 PM to 6:00 PM, from east to west. However, this

time coincides with the time when the Public Works Bureau staff go to and from the office, so this measure is actually for the convenience of the Public Works Bureau staff and not for the convenience of citizens and travelers. We should request your committee to negotiate and achieve the purpose of cancellation,

to protect the commercial safety of this road," etc., was received by the committee. According to the businesses, the Public Works Bureau's designation of Hankou Road traffic as one-way is only convenient for the Bureau staff to travel within the specified time and has no relation to the traffic of the entire city. On the contrary, the business operations on the road have been affected by this.

Therefore, this measure is not necessary for public transportation and is detrimental to business

operations. According to the principle of municipal facilities serving the welfare of the majority of citizens, we propose that your bureau abolish the method of changing Hankou Road traffic to one-way, so as to comply with public opinion and to maintain public friendship. Respectfully addressed to the Shanghai Municipal Council of the International Settlement.

After the project is completed, this unsanitary and unsightly canal will be eliminated. can largely offset the expenses incurred.

Leaflets Also Being Distributed in Wusong 176

In recent days, reactionary leaflets have been found from time to time on the outer Ma Road and railway station in Wusong. Therefore, the Seventh District Public Security Bureau and the First Chief of the Seventh District Police Station are paying close attention. At around 5:00 PM the day before yesterday, three students were distributing leaflets near the Huafeng Yarn Factory when they were spotted by patrolling police. As the police were about to step forward to arrest them,

the students immediately ran away quickly. The police chased after them, blowing their whistles wildly. At that time, it happened to be the time when the Yong'an and Huafeng Yarn Factories were letting out workers, and there were many workers coming and going. The female workers were panicked because they did not know the reason and fled in droves. The students fled to the east side of the Huafeng Factory and then turned north into a small road. They did not know that the road turned east and was the location of the First Police Station of the Seventh District. At that time, the chiefs and police officers of the station heard the sound of the whistles and came out to investigate, seeing three people running straight towards them. They stepped forward to intercept them,

and seized more than 100 reactionary leaflets in red, green, and yellow.

Chief Zhang Jiguang interrogated the students, who identified themselves as Zhou Jue, 19 years old, from Hunan, Liu Cong, 18 years old, from Changzhou, and Liang Hongqing, 19 years old, from Jiangxi. All three were students at Tongji University. All denied distributing leaflets. After a brief interrogation by Chief Zhang, they were immediately transferred to the Third Branch of the Judiciary. After a preliminary interrogation by Section Chief Chen, because it was related to politics, a document was prepared and sent to the Judicial Section of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau for interrogation and verification.

The Last Gamble 178

Chen Ding's Addiction to Flower Gambling

Pledge Ticket Shows Determination

Chen Ding, a Ningbo woman who used to live in Dexing Lane, North Zhejiang Road,

was nearly forty years old. Her husband died, leaving behind a son who was being raised at his maternal grandparents' home in Hongkou. Chen was friendly with Zhao Qin Huai and his wife in the same lane and often said to Zhao that she had more than a thousand yuan from uncollected gambling debts, which she would entrust to Zhao to invest at high

interest rates. However, Chen was addicted to gambling, especially flower gambling, which left her penniless. She had borrowed more than a hundred yuan at high interest rates from Zhao, which she had not repaid. Later, she continued to ask Zhao's wife to borrow fifty yuan (at an interest rate of 2,500 cash per day). Zhao was happy to help because he believed that Chen had more than a thousand yuan of uncollected gambling debts to rely on. Who knew that Chen would disappear without a trace. Zhao and his wife searched everywhere but could not find her. Unexpectedly, Zhao suddenly encountered Chen on a trolleybus on the 18th Road the other day.

It was indeed an enemy meeting on a narrow road. Chen said to Zhao that she was going to Ningbo for business

and was now planning to come to settle the debt. They went together to Zhao's home, where they calculated that she owed more than four hundred yuan in principal and interest. She promised to go with him to her mother's house the next day to get the money and then stayed at Zhao's house. Zhao believed

it to be true. Unexpectedly, Chen opened the door and fled in the middle of the night. When Zhao and his wife woke up, she was already gone like a yellow crane. The next day, Zhao went to Chen's mother's

house and asked. Chen's brother said that he had already repaid more than a thousand yuan on Chen's behalf, because she

had not changed her gambling habits and had already declared a break in relations. Zhao could not force him and had to go home. Unexpectedly, on the afternoon of the same day, Zhao received a letter sent by Chen Ding by mail, along with a pledge ticket. The letter said that she had now pledged six or seventy yuan and was going to make a final attempt to win a jackpot at the French Concession flower gambling den. Please inquire and see if it would land on the intended number. If so, both of them would benefit. If heaven does not bless me, I will have to throw myself into the Huangpu River to repay you in the next life. Please send the pledge ticket to a certain place, as it was borrowed jewelry pledged for money to use as capital. Zhao and his wife were shocked and angry when they saw the letter and are now searching everywhere and reporting the letter to Chen's mother's house.

Verdict on the Case of Worker's Tragic Death 179

Yang Kunlin, a carbide worker at the Yufa Chang Machine Factory at No. 23 O'Galou, was working with his colleague Ni Laofu on the morning of the other day when the electricity inside the carbide lamp was too strong, causing the small iron cylinder inside to pop out and strike Yang in the face, causing serious injuries.

As a result, he died. The Harbin patrol房 learned of this and ordered detectives to send Yang's body to the coroner's office on Ferron Road for examination. Yesterday morning, the Special District Local Court appointed Prosecutor Guo Wei to visit the office to examine the body and ascended to the public seat. According to Ni Laofu's report, the factory owner Yuan A'er, from Wuxi, also reported that Yang was indeed a worker in his factory, but according to regulations, he should have brought the work home and should not have worked in the factory, so he could not be held responsible for compensation.

Yang Zhang, the deceased's wife, said, "My husband's work can only be done in the factory, because our home only has small machines, and the large machines are only in the factory. I request that the factory be ordered to pay appropriate compensation." Prosecutor Guo obtained the confession and ruled, "It is verified that the deceased Yang Kunlin died from being struck by an electrical cylinder. His wife, Yang Zhang, is ordered to provide a guarantee to claim the body for burial, and the factory is ordered to provide compensation."

Xujiahui Public Slaughterhouse

Request for Water Relief Measures 180

The meat merchants of Zhouxiangtai and others in Xujiahui Town, West Shanghai, specifically requested the Health Bureau to establish a public slaughter company in the town for the convenience of inspection, and repeatedly requested the installation of water pipes, but this was not done. Yesterday, they specifically sent a letter to the Town Business Association requesting that it be forwarded to the Health Bureau, stating, "Since the meat merchants in West Shanghai (Xujiahui Caohejing Longhua) have been concentrated in this slaughterhouse and inspection after slaughter has been implemented, the number of slaughtered animals has gradually increased daily, and the relationship between water usage is important. Businessmen have repeatedly requested installation of water pipes, but they have not been installed. If river water is used, the Zhaojia Bang River will become increasingly clogged, and the water in the river is not only black and smelly, but sometimes it is difficult to find a drop of water. There is no other place to take water from. Although we are forced to use sewage, it is extremely unsanitary. If we need to dig an artesian well, there is no location or funding, and the difficult situation has reached its extreme. We are specifically requesting that your association promptly forward the request for immediate relief measures to maintain business and emphasize sanitation."

Appeal of Woman's Case to Divide Family Property 181

The Plaintiff Lost in the First Instance

The Appeal Has Concluded Its Arguments

Zhang Jinbao and her sister, Zhang Gennan, women from this county, previously hired a lawyer in the Provisional Court to file a civil lawsuit against their stepmother, Zhang Pu, for not dividing their deceased father's estate. After a preliminary hearing, the plaintiff lost the case. Zhang Jinbao and others, dissatisfied with the first instance judgment, hired a lawyer to file an appeal. Yesterday afternoon at 2 PM, Hu Yigu, the Presiding Judge of the Civil Division of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, along with Judges Han Zuzhi and Ye Zaiyi, ascended to the court to hold a hearing. Both parties arrived with their lawyers. Zhang Jinbao stated, "I am a local, 27 years old, and live on Yidingpan Road.

I am engaged, but not yet married. My father's name is Yu Sun, and my biological mother, Lu, died many years ago. She had two daughters. The appellant Zhang Pu is my stepmother and has two sons. My father passed away in 1925, leaving behind land and other property worth approximately 60,000 to 70,000 yuan.

Although my stepmother gave me 1,000 yuan for dowry last year, my sisters and I want to divide the family property equally with the two brothers, and my wardrobe and other belongings have been embezzled. I am currently living with my maternal grandmother in Chadaikou, and

my livelihood is also uncertain." The appellant Zhang Pu stated, "I am a local, 33 years old, and live at No. 502 at the end of Maigen Road. I have been married to Zhang Yu Sun for nine years and have two sons, one eight years old and the other six years old. My husband died in 1925, leaving behind more than 130 mu of rice fields in Lujia Bang, Kunshan, and six or seven mu of real estate in Shanghai, totaling approximately 12,000 to 20,000 yuan, which I manage. However, all of Yu Sun's previous wife's jewelry is held by Jinbao. Last year, Jinbao wanted to get married and asked me for money, so I gave her 1,200 yuan. However, after receiving the money, she filed a lawsuit. As for the second daughter, Gennan, if she still recognizes me as her mother,

I am willing to raise her. When she gets married in the future, I will give her dowry money. Moreover, my two sons are still young and cannot divide the family property equally," etc. After the arguments by the lawyers of both parties, Judge Hu ruled that the arguments in this case were concluded and the verdict would be announced on April 16.

Old Woman from Qingpu Committed Suicide by Poison 182

Zhang, an old woman from Qingpu, 58 years old this year, went alone to the Hexing Inn at No. 52 Mintini Road, French Concession, on the evening of the 9th to borrow a bed. For some unknown reason, she suddenly had a negative thought and committed suicide by swallowing raw opium. It was not until she moaned in pain from the poison that

Yu Shaofu, the teahouse waiter at the inn, learned of it. He immediately reported it to the Songshan Road patrol房 and ordered detectives to send her by car to Renji Hospital. However, the poison in her abdomen was too deep, and the rescue was ineffective. She died yesterday morning. The hospital notified the patrol房, who sent the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall coroner's office. There were no family members found. The patrol房 reported it to French Concession Judge Zhu Cheng at noon to examine the body. The judge confirmed that the deceased died from taking poison before death and ordered that photos be taken. The remains were collected and buried by the hall, awaiting family members to claim them.

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter 186

— Sea Guest

Bird Seller: Sir, would you like to buy this parrot? It can speak well and is very lively.

Henpecked Man: I already have a wife at home who speaks well, chattering at me day and night. It's lively enough.

A: Lao Bing is a poor fellow. He should marry a thrifty and hardworking wife.

B: Wrong. Precisely because he's a poor fellow,

he must marry a wealthy and powerful wife.

Astronomy Teacher: Do you know which star has a tail?

A Student: Ling Ding Ding (a type of firework).

Girl A: Would you be willing to marry a wasteful spendthrift in the future?

Girl B: It depends on how he spends. If he can't spend extravagantly for me, then I wouldn't want to marry him.

Girl A: I'm in a terrible situation these days. I don't know what to do.

Girl B: What's going on?

Girl A: My fiancé has broken up with me. He insists that I return his engagement ring. But I have many identical engagement rings in my jewelry box. I can't tell which one is his.

The West Lake of the Future 187

— Yan Qian

I once heard a revolutionary party member angrily say, "West Lake must be filled in!" Presumably, someone engaged in revolution loved to visit West Lake, neglecting their duties, which provoked this angry remark. Furthermore, I often hear people describe West Lake as intoxicating. In reality, this is not only insufficient to describe West Lake, but also insults it.

West Lake's beauty has its own unique aspects. It's not a matter of whether it intoxicates or not. In my opinion, since West Lake existed, there must have been people who visited it and failed to fully describe its beauty, but exclaimed, "West Lake is intoxicating!" As a result, West Lake has been mistakenly regarded by some as only capable of intoxicating.

On April 1st of this year, the National Congress of the Three Principles of the People was held on the shores of West Lake. I immediately felt a strong and heroic atmosphere filling the beautiful scenery, which could shake the minds of those who love to make noise, those who are intoxicated year-round, and those who have the despairing notion of living in a drunken dream, and dispel their absurd notion that West Lake is intoxicating.

From now on, I hope that those who visit West Lake will no longer be misled by the idea of intoxication and pretend to be elegant by getting drunk. I hope that those who visit West Lake will see the clear ripples and imagine the purity and health of the athletes, and understand that sports can lead to strength. See the towering Twin Peaks and imagine the tall and long-lived athletes, imagine the athletes' spirit full of beauty, and understand that sports are the fundamental art of achieving beauty. Only in this way can one live up to West Lake and avoid a meaningless visit.

Furthermore, one can deeply understand the ultimate meaning of holding the first National Congress of the Three Principles of the People in West Lake.

When the author submitted this article to Free Talk, he deeply wished that the people of the country would understand the importance of sports in the future and achieve the goals of freedom and equality through this. Then, those who visit the lake in the future may recall my humble self because of Free Talk. A smile.

Grass Flowers of Wu Palace 188

— Yi Mei

Stealing leisure from a busy schedule, I returned home for ten days. I recorded a few of the more interesting things I heard and saw.

As follows:

Gu Heyi, the painting master, is as famous as the late Lu Lianfu for his landscapes. The price of his paintings is several times higher than Lu's. Often, even a small fan or album leaf costs forty or fifty gold. Even those who offer high commissions and seek his work cannot obtain it without repeated requests.

This is because he has many unfinished pieces and sometimes makes forgeries of ancient works, selling them for hundreds or thousands of gold, which is not uncommon. Therefore, instead of creating his own works, he would rather create ancient works, sell them for a good price, and then profit from them. Unexpectedly, he suddenly suffered a stroke last month. With the help of medicine, he managed to survive.

However, he is now paralyzed and can no longer engage in painting. What a pity.

In the past, there was a seller of Zhuangyuan cakes. He was originally from a noble family, lost his fortune to a courtesan named Jin Feng, and became addicted to opium, eventually becoming a humble vendor. He also loved alcohol, and after drinking, he would often tell people about his past romantic affairs, which listeners used as a laughingstock. This spring, he suddenly fell ill and died in his sleep. His remains were collected by the famous painter Wu Zishen, which was truly a meritorious act.

Random Notes on Reading Paintings at Qingfeng Mingyue Cottage 189

— Wang Mei Xue

Qingfeng Mingyue Cottage is the residence of Mr. Xu Qianfu on Avenue Road in the French Concession of Shanghai. My friend Shen Shijia recently came from the West Lake and lives here. My old friend Wang Qianlou also came to Shanghai, both responding to the demands of Shanghai residents and making a living through painting. Qianfu is a refined scholar, so he is happy to recruit them.

However, Qianlou has another residence and only comes here occasionally to paint.

Last Sunday "April 6th," I visited Qianfu's residence at 2:00 PM to visit Shijia for a half-day chat. Qianlou also happened to be there. Both gentlemen are skilled in landscape painting. On that day, I saw screens, wall hangings, square paintings, and horizontal scrolls on display, almost covering all the famous mountains and rivers, giving a sense of being detached from the world. Finally, each showed me a small painting. Qianlou painted pine trees and inscribed them with my nickname. The bark was weathered, the branches strong,

resembling a thousand-year-old tree. How could I surpass it? Shijia painted a landscape with a sense of openness that struck my brow, and he inscribed a five-character poem expressing his deep feelings. He was especially able to move between Tao Yuanming and Han Yu. His poem said, "Where does the clear whistle sound? Gazing afar at the deep woods. Above the desolate stream and green clouds, the sounds of luan and phoenix are faint. Grass and stones have no names, and the rocks and springs are also silent. May I ask what year is this? The heavens are drunk and have not yet awakened." I was immersed in it, reluctant to let go. Qianlou suddenly asked, "Who is Meng Yu? Is he your friend?" I said, "Yes, so why are you teasing me so much?" Then he took out Meng Yu's article "Colorful Phoenixes Fly to the West" from the Free Talk of that day and pointed it out, saying, "This article mentions Miss Mei Qu and her son Yunhua. Meng Yu probably thinks that your daughter has a masculine air, so he doesn't call her a daughter but a son. He must also think that you don't have a masculine air, so he calls you a lady." Everyone laughed. I said,

"If Meng Yu didn't make this bad joke, it must be a mistake by the typesetter. It's just a coincidence. However, I am willing to exchange my hairpin and hat with my daughter and deeply thank the typesetter for resolving this dispute." Everyone asked, "Is there an explanation?" I said, "Yes. My daughter's name is Yunhua, and I have another female disciple named Yunhua, also surnamed Wang. They both study painting and have different approaches. Three years ago, Meng Yu, the editor of Camel Painting News, made a statement

saying, "Wang Yunhua of Wu, the female disciple of Mei Qu, and Wang Yunhua of Lingnan, the daughter of Mei Qu." However, those who see their works in Shanghai and Hangzhou still suspect that they are counterfeit copies. Mr. and Mrs. Xu Shiqi invited us to dinner the other day and suspected that my daughter, who usually studies Western painting, was the one who paints female figures. Mrs. Xu, Yang Manhua, suspected it even more.

Now that the typesetter made a mistake and my daughter exchanged her hairpin for a hat, it can be known that she is definitely not Yunhua of Wu, who paints landscapes. As for the aging Mei Qu, it doesn't matter whether you call him a horse or a cow." Everyone was smiling. A guest came to visit and asked what school Shijia's painting belonged to. Qianfu replied,

"His painting style is thick and has a scholarly air. He has worked hard on the styles of Yuan Shanjiao and Tao Dachai, and his source comes from the Four Wangs. He is able to avoid being restricted by the Four Wangs." The guest nodded. I was also fortunate to hear the secrets of the painter. I hastily wrote this as random notes on reading paintings.

Newspaper Quilt 190

— Xu Xiaoting

Newspapers are a medium for advertising and news. After reading them, except for a few literati who keep them, people usually use them to wrap copper coins or paste them on walls. I have never heard of them being used for other purposes. However, a certain Feng in Huaiyin actually made a quilt out of newspapers to protect his body temperature, which is truly unexpected.

Feng is over seventy years old and extremely poor, but he is addicted to reading this newspaper. He has no possessions, but he has accumulated decades' worth of newspapers. The newspaper can only be used to impart knowledge, not to make money. When Feng sleeps, he only has a single thin quilt to cover himself. Last winter, the weather was extremely cold. Feng was attacked by the cold and his body was as cold as iron. He had a strange idea. He took out the old newspapers from the shelf and spread them out. He glued each sheet together, making several sheets. The length and width were similar to his body. Then he pasted over a hundred sheets in the same way, stacked them in a pile, and connected them with thread. When it was finished, it was no different from a quilt. Feng took it and wrapped it around his body. It was much warmer than covering himself with a single thin quilt.

Feng told people the other day that he had been using this quilt for several months.

The parts that touch the body feel a little unclean. Just tear off a layer, and it will be clean again. In the spring, the weather changed from extremely cold to warm.

The layers of my quilt were torn off one by one, changing from thick to thin. It doesn't need to be washed, and it's suitable for the weather. Poor scholars of the world,

if you can follow my example, then those cotton wads and quilts

will be useless.

The above facts were told to me by my friend Huang Yinmin.

This newspaper has opened up a new use. This strange and interesting event is truly amusing.

Anecdotes of Red Apricots 191

— Zheng Yimei

The warm air is quietly urging the new blossoms of apricot flowers. This is truly a great adornment of spring. The flowers and leaves of the apricot are similar to those of the plum. It is a deciduous small tree. The fruit is yellow and ripe, sweet but not sour. The kernels can be mashed into juice.

It can treat coughs. This is why the ancients had the saying, "Don't say that the fruit is for people to eat, the broken kernels can still be used as medicine." Miscellaneous Records of Youyang: Southeast of Jinan County, there is Fenliu Mountain, which has many apricots, as large as pears and as yellow as oranges, called Hanwu Apricots. However, when asked about it, the people of Lu all said they had never heard of it. Presumably, the fine variety has long been extinct. The method of planting apricots is to bury the kernels with the flesh in manure soil and transplant them in the spring. Otherwise, the fruit will be small and bitter. It is best to plant them near people's homes and not too densely. If they are too dense, the flowers will be sparse and the fruit will be few. Gardeners must know this.

My fellow student Jin Jihe's respected father, He Wangzhang, has been a sojourner in Wu for many years. He lives in Mr. Fei Weizhai's house, which has a red apricot tree that is tall, beautiful, and pleasing. In the past, during the flowering season, Zhang moved to Xinqiao Lane. However, because the red apricots were so beautiful, he could not move them together with his zither, wine, books, and paintings. He was quite regretful about this. The calligrapher and painter Bi Xungu knew this,

so he painted a large branch of apricot blossoms and named it "The Marrying Apricot Picture" as a gift. Zhang wrote a long poem about it, which was passed down as a beautiful story for a time. According to "The Marrying Apricot,"

it has been around since ancient times. Miscellaneous Records of Wenchang: The apricot tree in front of Li Guanqing's hall had many flowers but no fruit. A matchmaker smiled and said, "Next spring, I will marry this apricot." In the depth of winter, she suddenly brought wine and asked for a virgin's skirt to tie to the tree, offered a blessing, and left. The following spring, it bore countless fruits. This story is almost absurd and is only for amusement.

Zhang Yunhe, a famous painter in Shanghai, lived with his patron, Dan Jinyu. Because I was familiar with Zhang, I asked him to paint a picture of apricot forest spring swallows. After it was completed, Zhang suddenly discovered that in the midst of the dense flowers, the fluttering swallows

were exactly eight in number. Fearing that he would be laughed at by vulgar people, he remade a painting to replace it. I took it back, but Dan Jinyu was not offended by the eight swallows and kept it carefully. As a result, I also managed to seize one of them.

I was quite fortunate about it.

In Western restaurants, there is a dish called almond tofu, which is made with almonds in tofu, mixed with sugar syrup, and stored in the refrigerator. It is sweet and delicious and is a good product for cooling off in the summer.

Good stories of apricots are often seen in ancient books, such as Confucius resting on the apricot altar, and Dong Feng living in Mount Lu, treating people for illnesses, planting five apricot trees for serious cases and one tree for minor cases, known as Dong Xian's Apricot Forest. Also, Guo Ziyi crossed the river from Apricot Garden to surround Weizhou, with the Apricot Garden crossing site.

Also, Song Qi had the line "Red apricot branch head spring meaning riot," and was then called Red Apricot Secretary. Also, the immortal Liu Gen hid in Apricot Mountain, and the Shanglin Garden had Penglai Apricots, which were offered by Dong Hai Duwei Yu Ji.

Good poems about apricots include "Drunk in the jade building under apricot flowers," "Plum blossoms have faded, apricot blossoms are new," "Selling apricot flowers in deep alleys tomorrow morning," "Apricot buds like faces, half-open and fragrant," "Apricot branches leaning and flowers swaying," "Thousands of red apricot trees in front of the Wenxing Hall," "Famous gardens leaning against each other, apricot flowers blooming," "Girls pick them with care, saying it is the flower of the spring breeze and passing the exam," "Powder is thin, red is light, covering shame, occupying the limelight among flowers," "Ashamed to meet the willow eyes, three points of white, dividing the peach cheeks, a smiling red." The beauty is endless.

Warmth in the Heart (168) 192

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 10: The Red Flame Soars to the Sky, the Balcony Admires the Filial Daughter; the Red Carpet is Laid Out, a Famous Actor is Met on the Spot

But in that scene... the female lead, the prodigal lady... was driven out of her home... suffering from terminal tuberculosis... and remembering her husband... many ladies and wives in the whole theatre... were shedding tears there... even to the point of sobbing faintly... Zuo Shichen turned his head and looked at Ruiyun... whose eyes were already red... even Ah Jin was wiping her tears there... Ruiyun wasn't wiping her eyes at this moment... but just rubbing her nose with her handkerchief... Zuo Shichen said... "How is it... are you crying too... hey... this is just acting... it's not real..." Ruiyun said... "Knowing it's acting... I still feel sad for her..." As she said that... her voice was also a little choked up... Zuo Shichen said... "This is bad... I invited you to see a play... originally to find happiness... now it's causing you to shed tears... bringing on sadness... that's not good... let's not watch the following scene... let's go back..." Ruiyun said... "No... I'll watch it all and then go..." Zuo Shichen said... "The following scene... is also material for tears... it's her husband... injured in battle... in the hospital... getting news of his beloved wife... this is originally a tragedy... with no good ending... let's go back... let's save the tears for the next scene..." Zuo Shichen stood up to leave... but Ruiyun held him down with one hand... and said... "No, no... I must watch it all before I go..."

"The more it brings tears... the more I want to watch... is this kind of thing really happening... or is it all made up by them... to cheat people out of their tears..." Zuo Shichen held Ruiyun's hand tightly and said... "In that case, I'll teach you not to watch... so you don't get cheated out of your tears... why aren't you willing..." Ruiyun said... "I myself don't know... I just want to watch... they act so realistically... making people forget that they are acting..." At that time, it wasn't just Ruiyun who was shedding tears... seeing the sad parts... many people were shedding tears... especially those wives and ladies... It wasn't until the whole play was finished... that everyone dispersed and went home... At this time, as everyone stood up... Ah Jin suddenly remembered... and said... "Today, Anan's luck... there were probably a few round songs... Big Aunt asked people to fill in... why didn't any of the round song singers come..." "It's probably because you, Second Young Master, explained it thoroughly to Big Aunt..." Ruiyun stood up... gently stretched... and said... "That's right... I forgot too... I got dizzy watching the play... and forgot about the round songs... they really didn't come to sing..." Zuo Shichen said... "I knew they wouldn't come..." Ruiyun said... "Why not..." Zuo Shichen nodded and said... "That's why he said he wanted to come and sing that day...

I readily agreed with him... Let me ask you... has your assistance ever been to this place..." Ah Jin said... "Never been..." Zuo Shichen said... "Never been... I can't find this place either... even if I find it... the Indian doorman at the door won't let him in... unless he has a ticket... This theatre isn't like those old theatres... where anyone can run in... so even if they want to sing round songs... they can't run in..."

First Comparison Period After Calendar Change Is Busy 196

Market Overview: The silver and money industry has always valued the lunar calendar. At this time, it coincided with the particularly busy third month of the lunar calendar's special comparison period. According to reason, the momentum should be unusually strong. This year, the national calendar is used, and it is designated as April. Therefore, yesterday was also the first of the busiest great comparison period. Since the change to the national calendar, it has been a creation. Looking at the prosperity of inflows and outflows, although not as good as last year, compared to the usual collection and disbursement,

there is a great difference. Therefore, the demand for silver loans is special, and foreign loans are also due to fewer customer routes for consumption, showing no weakness. The combination of the two resulted in an unusually busy scene.

Yarn and Cotton Yarn Prices Turned Good in the Afternoon

The yarn market fell in the morning and rose in the afternoon, with a firmer trend. Overseas cotton yarn was stable.

A certain manufacturer searched for a large amount of near-month futures. On the one hand, they transported the yarn in the yarn warehouse to other ports and there was also manufacturer assistance. Therefore, the buyers' courage was particularly strong, and the market situation was tightened by them. It was difficult to fall for a while, but the short attitude was still firm.
